\newcommand{\cmark}{\ding{51}}
\newcommand{\xmark}{\ding{55}}
\newcommand{\fastkernels}{FastKernels}
\begin{document}

\section*{HF Transformers $\to$ \fastkernels{} per-class kernel mapping (full audit)}

\noindent
\textbf{Status legend:} $\bullet$ kb-nano L4 pipeline ships; \cmark{} every kernel exists, only L4 wiring remains; \textbf{P} partial; \xmark{} unsupported.

\textbf{Mapping legend:} \texttt{L<n>/file.py} -- the class has its own kernel and maps directly to that file. \textit{A + B + C} -- the class is implemented by the listed kb-nano files combined (no exact single match). \textit{n$\times$file.py} indicates the same kernel is invoked multiple times within the class.
